##random_list_list Discipline and Trait generation by Preacher
###Start up character creation
namespace = TOSDTG

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.1

	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		min_age = 16
		OR = {
			culture_group = north_germanic
			culture_group = central_germanic
			culture_group = west_germanic
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = dalmatian
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = celtic
			culture_group = finno_ugric
			culture_group = baltic
			culture_group = altaic
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = levantine_arabic
			culture_group = east_slavic
			culture_group = west_slavic
			culture_group = south_slavic
			culture_group = magyar
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = east_african
			culture_group = west_african
			culture_group = mesoamerican
			culture_group = israelite
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
			culture_group = vasconic
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = character_creation }
	}
	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = athletic_dicispline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_arts_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = military_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = scholarly_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_stewardship_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = knowledge_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = criminal_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = spycraft_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = animal_handling_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = arts_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = medicine_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = sciences_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = learning_scholarly_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = theology_discipline value = 1 }
		
	character_event = { id = TOSDTG.2 }
	
	set_character_flag = character_creation
		
	}
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.2 
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	weight_multiplier = { days = 1 }	
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				is_variable_equal = { which = discipine value = 1 }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 1 }
				}
				30 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 2 }
				}
				20 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 3 }
				}
				10 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 4 }
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.3 } 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}
	
character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.3
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 1 }
			}
			create_character = {
				random_list_list_traits = no 
				dynasty =  random_list_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.4 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 2 }
			}
			create_character = {
				random_list_list_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 2 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.4 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 3 } 
			}
			create_character = {
				random_list_list_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 3 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.4 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 4 } 
			}
			create_character = {
				random_list_list_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			new_character = {
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 4 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.4 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.4
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 1 }
		is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 2 }
		is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 3 }
		is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 4 }
		
		OR = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				random_list = {
					5 = {
						modifier = {
							NOT = { 
								has_character_flag = athletic_dicispline 
							}
						}
						is_variable_equal = { which = athletic_dicispline value = 1 }

	id = TOSDTG.40
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
			OR = {
				any_playable_ruler = {

						14 = {

						}

						}
						14 = {
							add_trait = leadership_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }

							add_trait = siege_engines_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						14 = {

							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }

					}
				}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.41
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 2 }
			OR = {
				any_playable_ruler = {
					random_list = {
						7 = {
							modifier = {
								NOT = { 
									trait = armoury_II 
								}
							}
							add_trait = armoury_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }

								NOT = {

								}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.46
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
			OR = {
				any_playable_ruler = {
					add_trait = public_speaking_I
					subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				}
				any_courtier = {
					add_trait = public_speaking_I
					subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				}
				any_vassal = {
					add_trait = public_speaking_I
					subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay 
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.55
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
			OR = {
				any_playable_ruler = {
					random_list = {
						16 = {
							add_trait = disguise_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = fast_talk_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = forced_entry_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = observation_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = smuggling_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = streetwise_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				any_courtier = {
					random_list = {
						16 = {
							add_trait = disguise_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = fast_talk_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = forced_entry_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = observation_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = smuggling_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = streetwise_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				any_vassal = {
					random_list = {
						16 = {
							add_trait = disguise_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = fast_talk_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = forced_entry_I
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = observation_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
						}
						16 = {
							add_trait = smuggling_I 
							subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }

						16 = {

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.61		#formerly 52
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
		or = {
		any_playable_ruler = {
			random_list = {
			50 = {
				add_trait = falconer_I 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
			}
			50 = {
				add_trait = warhorse_I 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
			}
		}
		}
		any_vassal = {

				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
			}

				add_trait = martial_cleric
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = detached_priest
					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = mastermind_theologian
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = scholarly_theologian
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = martial_cleric
					trait = detached_priest
					trait = mastermind_theologian
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = mastermind_theologian
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = martial_cleric
					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = detached_priest
				}
			}
		}
		}
		any_vassal = {
		random_list = {
			12 = {
				add_trait = philosophy_I 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = philosophy_II
					trait = philosophy_III
					trait = philosophy_IV
				}
			}
			12 = {

##Character creation during game play

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.85
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		min_age = 16
		OR = {
			culture_group = north_germanic
			culture_group = central_germanic
			culture_group = west_germanic
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = dalmatian
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = celtic
			culture_group = finno_ugric
			culture_group = baltic
			culture_group = altaic
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = levantine_arabic
			culture_group = east_slavic
			culture_group = west_slavic
			culture_group = south_slavic
			culture_group = magyar
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = east_african
			culture_group = west_african
			culture_group = mesoamerican
			culture_group = israelite
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
			culture_group = vasconic
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = character_creation }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = { days = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = athletic_dicispline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_arts_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = military_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = scholarly_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_stewardship_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = knowledge_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = criminal_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = spycraft_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = animal_handling_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = arts_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = medicine_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = sciences_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = learning_scholarly_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = theology_discipline value = 1 }
		
	character_event = { id = TOSDTG.77 } }
	
	set_character_flag = character_creation
		
	}
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.86
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				is_variable_equal = { which = discipine value = 1 }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 1 }
				}
				30 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 2 }
				}
				20 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 3 }
				}
				10 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 4 }
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.78 } }
		}
		
		weight_multiplier = { days = 1 }	
	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}
	
character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.87
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 1 }
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = no 
				dynasty =  random_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.79 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 2 }
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 2 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.80 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 3 } 
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 3 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.81 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_equal = { which = traits value = 4 } 
			}
			create_character = {
				random_traits = no
				dynasty =  random_list
				culture =  ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				set_variable = { which = traits value = 4 }
			}
			character_event = { id = TOSDTG.82 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

####random_list Discipline and Trait Assignment to existing characters.
character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.160
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		min_age = 16
		any_playable_ruler = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = north_germanic
				culture_group = central_germanic
				culture_group = west_germanic
				culture_group = latin
				culture_group = dalmatian
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = celtic
				culture_group = finno_ugric
				culture_group = baltic
				culture_group = altaic
				culture_group = arabic
				culture_group = levantine_arabic
				culture_group = east_slavic
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = magyar
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = east_african
				culture_group = west_african
				culture_group = mesoamerican
				culture_group = israelite
				culture_group = indo_aryan_group
				culture_group = dravidian_group
				culture_group = vasconic
			}
		}
		any_province_character = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = north_germanic
				culture_group = central_germanic
				culture_group = west_germanic
				culture_group = latin
				culture_group = dalmatian
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = celtic
				culture_group = finno_ugric
				culture_group = baltic
				culture_group = altaic
				culture_group = arabic
				culture_group = levantine_arabic
				culture_group = east_slavic
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = magyar
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = east_african
				culture_group = west_african
				culture_group = mesoamerican
				culture_group = israelite
				culture_group = indo_aryan_group
				culture_group = dravidian_group
				culture_group = vasconic
			}
			set_character_flag = character_creation
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = character_creation }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = { days = 1 }
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = athletic_dicispline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_arts_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = military_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = scholarly_diplomacy_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = business_stewardship_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = knowledge_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = criminal_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = spycraft_discpline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = animal_handling_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = arts_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = weapon_design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = design_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = medicine_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = sciences_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = learning_scholarly_discipline value = 1 }
		set_variable = { which = theology_discipline value = 1 }
		
	character_event = { id = TOSDTG.152 } }
	
	set_character_flag = character_creation
		
	}
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.161
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				is_variable_equal = { which = discipine value = 1 }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 1 }
					character_event = { id = TOSDTG.162 } }
				}
				30 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 2 }
					character_event = { id = TOSDTG.163 } }
				}
				20 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 3 }
					character_event = { id = TOSDTG.164 } }
				}
				10 = {
					set_variable = { which = traits value = 4 }
					character_event = { id = TOSDTG.165 } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		weight_multiplier = { days = 1 }	
	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = Okay
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.166
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			45 = {
				add_trait = athletics_I
				NOT = {
					trait = athletics_II
					trait = athletics_III
					trait = athletics_IV
				}
			}
			25 = {
				add_trait = athletics_II
				NOT = {
					trait = athletics_I
					trait = athletics_III
					trait = athletics_IV
				}
				set_variable = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
				character_event = { id = TOSDTG.183 } }
			}
			20 = {
				add_trait = athletics_III
				NOT = {
					trait = athletics_I
					trait = athletics_II
					trait = athletics_IV
				}
				set_variable = { which = subtraits value = 2 }
				character_event = { id = TOSDTG.184 } }
			}
			10 = {
				add_trait = athletics_IV
				NOT = {
					trait = athletics_I
					trait = athletics_II
					trait = athletics_III
				}
				set_variable = { which = subtraits value = 2 }
				character_event = { id = TOSDTG.185 } }

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.184
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 2 }
		random_list = {
			35 = {
				add_trait = manouvering_I
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
			}
			15 = { 
				add_trait = manouvering_II 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = { trait = manouvering_I }
			}
			35 = {
				add_trait = combat_arts_I
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
			}
			15 = {
				add_trait = combat_arts_II 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = { trait = combat_arts_I }
			}
		}

character_event = {
	id = TOSDTG.233
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		is_variable_equal = { which = subtraits value = 1 }
		
		random_list = {
			12 = {
				add_trait = philosophy_I 
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = philosophy_II
					trait = philosophy_III
					trait = philosophy_IV
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = philosophy_II
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = philosophy_I
					trait = philosophy_III
					trait = philosophy_IV
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = philosophy_III
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = philosophy_I
					trait = philosophy_II
					trait = philosophy_IV
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = philosophy_IV
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = philosophy_I
					trait = philosophy_II
					trait = philosophy_III
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = detached_priest
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = martial_cleric
					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = mastermind_theologian
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = martial_cleric
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = detached_priest
					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = mastermind_theologian
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = scholarly_theologian
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {

					trait = detached_priest
					trait = mastermind_theologian
				}
			}
			12 = {
				add_trait = mastermind_theologian
				subtract_variable = { which = subtraits value 1 }
				NOT = {
					trait = martial_cleric
					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = detached_priest
				}
			}
		}

	option = {
		name = Okay
